  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=5.7)
    The writing demonstrates some originality in its approach to symbolism and meaning, but suffers from occasional purple prose ("weathered hearts left her questioning her craft") and overly formal dialogue. The bee pin metaphor shows promise but feels somewhat predictable in execution. While the prose avoids the most obvious AI patterns, phrases like "the weight of unspoken stories hanging heavy in the air" read as generic literary flourishes rather than fresh insights. The characters' interactions lack the nuanced emotional complexity of truly distinctive fiction.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=5.4)

The story relies heavily on explicitly stating the character's feelings rather than revealing them through specific, unique reactions. The concept of recipes as emotional anchors is interesting but executed with somewhat predictable metaphors. The writing lacks a distinctive stylistic signature that would elevate it beyond competent genre fiction.
